 2011 se schuli shiksha main jansanchaar ke shaamil hone tathaa videshi vishvavidhyalayon kii desh main dastak ke maddenjar ypi uniwarsity ke media skool ne apni qamar kas lee he
 What can be the strategy to deal with future challenges, Professor In charge of IP University Chandrakant Prasad Singh is telling
 prashn- videshi vishvavidhyalayon ke bharat main aane se media skulon par kya prabhaav padegaa? uttar- videshi vishvavidhyalay apane saath anubhav, takanic tathaa visheshgyata lekar aaenge, aise main desh main maujuud vishvavidhyalayon ko bhi shiksha ke str main khaasaa sudhaar karnaa hoga or industry ke saath shiksha ko jodna hoga
 Q: What do you think these improvements can be? Answer - See, the biggest weakness of media university education is that it is not market oriented
 yahi kaaran he ki vishvavidhyalayon se training lekar aae bacchon ke prati industry kam utsukata dikhaati he
 This reform has to be done two-way
 pehla yah ki media skulon main padhaaye jane vaale course main vyapak parivartan karnaa hoga, taaki vah samaaj or bazaar kii jaruraton ko puraa kar sake or doosraa yah ranneetik hona chahie
 Q- What do you mean by strategy improvement? Answer- To say strategic means that improvement should be based on local needs, global challenges and opportunities
 aap bharat kii puraatan shiksha pranali ko dekh lijie
 Our history of better education system is old
 hamaare yahaan vishwa prasiddh nalanda vishvavidhyalay tha, jahaan vishvabhar se log shiksha praapt karne aate the, lekin samay ke saath hamaari shiksha vyavastha main giravat ai or or saath hi hamaara vikascram bhi baadhit hua
 Today, when we are on the path of development again, it is necessary that we make our education system fit and change according to the times, so that our development can continue, and the old image of Vishwa Guru which was India's That can be achieved
 prashn- agle saal se skulon main bhi media ko ek vishay ke rup main joda ja rahaa he
 In such a situation, what roadmap do you have for future needs? Answer: The addition of media as a subject in 11th and 12th schools in schools from 2011 also means that from 2013-14, about 7 lakh children would like to graduate in this subject at university level, so at least 40 thousand college teachers will be needed
 isliye samay rahete aane vaali chunautiyon kii taiyaari kar lenaa hi samajhadaari hogi or duuradrushti bhi
 Q: What do you see the future of media school in India? Answer: The growth rate of the media sector is 12 to 14 per cent annually, which is the highest after the telecom sector, so it cannot be sidelined
 darasal, media main shiksha kaa matlab zyaadaatar patrakarita se hi liya jaataa rahaa he, jabaki gaiyr patrakarita kshetra bhi utana hi mahatvapurn he, jisamen vigyaapan va jansanchaar, anemeshan, media management aadi aate hai
 Communication, a subject of media, is also taught by management students as a subject
 aane vaale samay main iskaa or failaav hoga or vyaktitv vikaas ke rup main isko sabhi profeshnal corson main shaamil kiya jayega
 So, according to me, the future of media school is bright
 prashn- lekin aap is baat ko to maanenge ki patrakarita bhi ek ahm kshetra he or ek ubhartee hui industry bhi
 So how will you find the distance of the university from the industry? Answer - You are absolutely right and i also fully respect this
 isliye hamane apane media skool ko industry se jodne ke liye ek cell kaa nirmaan kiya he, jisamen vishvavidhyalay ke shikshakon ke saath, industry se jude behtareen profeshnals honge
 Which will not only check the performance of the students here, but will also suggest changes in the course according to the needs of the industry
 prashn- bharat main ucch shiksha kii sabase badi kami yah rahi he ki hamaare yahaan shodh par bahut adhik jor nahin diya ja rahaa
 What is the media school of IP taking in this direction? Answer - Our Vice Chancellor Professor DK Bandopadhyay gives great importance to research and is a visionary
 yahi kaaran he ki hamane jald hi media shodh ko badhaane kaa faisla kiya he
 That is why we are going to start phd in Mass Communication in the coming 5-6 months, which has been approved
 itnaa hi nahin hamane masters level par bhi shodh par vyapak jor dene kaa faisla kiya he
 Students doing masters in media will have to submit three research papers, out of which two will be small and one will be detailed study
 iskaa sidhaa phayda yah hoga ki vidhyaarthiyon kaa rujhaan research kii taraf badhegaa or desh main kai media modelon kaa vikaas sambhav ho paaegaa
